\section{External states: ${e_{{i}}, \bar{e}_{{j}}, d_{{k}}, \bar{d}_{{l}}}$} 
\subsection{Wave contributions, Propagator: $Z$}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{A^0_{{a}}}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{A^0_{{a}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddSLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddVRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddTLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTRR= & 0 \\ 
\end{align}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{e_{{a}}}, m^2_{\delta^{c--}_{{b}}}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{e_{{a}}}, m^2_{\delta^{c--}_{{b}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddSLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddVRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddTLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTRR= & 0 \\ 
\end{align}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{H^-_{{b}}}) \\

  PVOllddSLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddVRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\nu e H^+,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\nu e H^+,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\nu e H^+,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{W^-}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{W^-}) \\ 
  PVOllddSLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddVRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^+,L}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^+,R}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^+,R}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^+,L}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^+,L}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^+,R}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^+,R}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^+,L}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddTLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTRR= & 0 \\ 
\end{align}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{W_R^-}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{W_R^-}) \\ 
  PVOllddSLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddVRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W_R^+,L}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W_R^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W_R^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W_R^+,R}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W_R^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W_R^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, c} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W_R^+,R}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W_R^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W_R^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W_R^+,L}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W_R^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W_R^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\

  PVOllddVRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{c, k} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, i} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\bar{d}u W_R^- ,L}_{l, b} m_{d_{{l}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,R}_{b, c} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{u_{{b}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,L}_{b, c} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{d_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{d}u W_R^- ,R}_{l, b} (\Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,R}_{b, c} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{d_{{l}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,L}_{b, c} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{u_{{b}}} m_{d_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{d_{{l}}} - m^2_{d_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{c, k} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, i} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\bar{d}u W_R^- ,R}_{l, b} m_{d_{{l}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,L}_{b, c} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{u_{{b}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,R}_{b, c} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{d_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{d}u W_R^- ,L}_{l, b} (\Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,L}_{b, c} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{d_{{l}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,R}_{b, c} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{u_{{b}}} m_{d_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{d_{{l}}} - m^2_{d_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,L}_{c, k} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,R}_{j, i} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\bar{d}u W_R^- ,R}_{l, b} m_{d_{{l}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,L}_{b, c} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{u_{{b}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,R}_{b, c} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{d_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{d}u W_R^- ,L}_{l, b} (\Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,L}_{b, c} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{d_{{l}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,R}_{b, c} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{u_{{b}}} m_{d_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{d_{{l}}} - m^2_{d_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddVLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{d}d Z ,R}_{c, k} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e Z ,L}_{j, i} \frac{1}{m^2_{Z}} (\Gamma^{\bar{d}u W_R^- ,L}_{l, b} m_{d_{{l}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,R}_{b, c} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{u_{{b}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,L}_{b, c} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{d_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{d}u W_R^- ,R}_{l, b} (\Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,R}_{b, c} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{d_{{l}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{u}d W_R^+,L}_{b, c} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{u_{{b}}} m_{d_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{d_{{l}}} - m^2_{d_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddTLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddTRR= & 0 \\ 
\end{align}

\subsection{Penguin contributions, Propagator: ${Z'}$} 



 \begin{center}
\begin{fmffile}{Diagrams/PengV2L2dPenguinNumberOfConsideredExternalStatesVZR1}

\begin{fmfgraph*}(150,75)

\fmflabel{$e_{{i}}$}{l2}

\fmflabel{$\bar{d}_{{l}}$}{r1}

\end{fmffile}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B0C0check(m^2_{e_{{c}}}, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{A^0_{{a}}}) \\ 
I_2= & C_{00}(m^2_{e_{{c}}}, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{A^0_{{a}}}) \\ 
I_3= & C_0(m^2_{e_{{c}}}, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{A^0_{{a}}}) \\ 
  PVOllddSLL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSRL= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddSLR= & 0 \\ 
  PVOllddVRR= &  \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{j, c, a} \Gamma^{\bar{d}d {Z'} ,R}_{l, k} \frac{1}{m^2_{{Z'}}} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}e {Z'} ,L}_{c, b} (I_1 - 2 I_2) - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e {Z'} ,R}_{c, b} I_3 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}) \\
